Output:
from __future__ import annotations

import asyncio
import json
import os
from pathlib import Path
from time import perf_counter

from crewai import Agent
from pydantic import BaseModel, Field

from automated_research_report_generator_v0_1.crew import get_llm
from automated_research_report_generator_v0_1.tools.pdf_page_tools import (
    PdfPageIndexEntry,
    build_page_index_payload,
    default_page_index_path,
    extract_pdf_pages,
    page_index_is_current,
    reset_pdf_page_tool_runtime_state,
    save_page_index,
    set_pdf_context,
)


# =========================
# Page Index Agent Parameters
# =========================

PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_ROLE = "PDF 逐页索引专员"  # 默认角色名；可改成更贴近你内部分工的中文称呼。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_GOAL = (  # 默认目标；可改成更强调“筛页”或“目录化索引”的版本。
    "逐页读取 PDF，并为每一页生成一个简短主题标签，帮助后续 agent 快速判断哪些页与自己的分析任务相关。"
)
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_BACKSTORY = (  # 默认背景设定；可改成更偏招股书、年报或行业报告场景。
    "你专门负责按页阅读 PDF。你不会跨页总结，也不会提前做整份文档分析。"
    "你的唯一职责是只根据当前这一页的内容，输出一个非常短、便于筛页的主题标签。"
)
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TEMPERATURE = 0.1  # 默认 0.1；可改到 0 更稳，0.2-0.3 会更灵活但更易漂移。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_VERBOSE = True  # 默认 True；调试时方便看 agent 过程，可改 False 收敛日志。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_ALLOW_DELEGATION = False  # 默认 False；该 agent 只做单页索引，不需要委派。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_REASONING = False  # 默认 False；该任务短且结构化，通常不需要额外 reasoning。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_CACHE = True  # 默认 True；相同输入可复用缓存，减少重复调用。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS = 20  # 逐页短调用不应该无限等到底层默认 600 秒。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_MAX_RETRIES = 0  # 单页失败直接走启发式兜底，避免一次卡住后再重试。


# =========================
# Page Index Task Parameters
# =========================

PAGE_INDEX_TOPIC_MAX_CHARS = 10  # 默认主题最长 10 字；可调大到 12-15 字换取更完整标签。
PAGE_INDEX_UNKNOWN_COMPANY = "未知公司"  # 默认公司占位值；上游没识别出公司时用于 prompt。
PAGE_INDEX_EMPTY_PAGE_TOPIC = "空白页"  # 默认空白页标签；可改成“扫描页”“图片页”等更贴近团队习惯的词。
PAGE_INDEX_FORCE_REBUILD_DEFAULT = False  # 默认优先复用缓存；改成 True 会每次都强制重建索引。
PAGE_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY_DEFAULT = 4  # 默认只开小并发，兼顾 OpenRouter 吞吐与稳定性。
PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_LIMIT_DEFAULT = 2  # 对 429、超时、网关波动做少量重试，避免瞬时抖动直接退化。
PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_BASE_DELAY_SECONDS = 2.0  # 并发场景下使用指数退避，给上游路由与限流一点缓冲时间。
PAGE_INDEX_PROMPT_RULES = (  # 默认任务规则；可逐条增删来调整主题标签风格。
    "只输出一个 `topic` 字段。",
    f"`topic` 最多 {PAGE_INDEX_TOPIC_MAX_CHARS} 个字。",
    "只关注当前这一页，不要总结整份文档。",
    "尽量使用具体的业务主题，不要使用空泛表述。",
    "如果本页主要是表格，就概括表格的主题。",
    "如果本页难以判断，就返回一个谨慎、简短的主题。",
    "不要输出解释、前后缀、Markdown 代码块或额外文本。",
)

# =========================
# Page Index Models
# =========================

class PageTopicSummary(BaseModel):
    topic: str = Field(..., description="当前页的简短主题标签")  # 单页主题字段，供后续 agent 快速筛页。


# =========================
# Page Index Helpers
# =========================

def _normalize_topic(topic: str, fallback: str) -> str:  # 清洗 LLM 或启发式产出的主题，统一成稳定短标签。
    normalized = " ".join((topic or "").split())
    normalized = normalized.replace('"', "").replace("'", "").replace("`", "").strip(" ,.;:()[]{}")
    compact = normalized.replace(" ", "").lower()
    if compact in {"json", "{", "}", "topic", "none", "null"}:
        normalized = ""
    if not normalized:
        normalized = fallback
    return normalized[:PAGE_INDEX_TOPIC_MAX_CHARS]


def _heuristic_topic(page_text: str, fallback: str) -> str:  # LLM 失败时退化为“取首个像标题的文本”。
    for line in page_text.splitlines():
        cleaned = " ".join(line.split()).strip(" ,.;:()[]{}")
        if len(cleaned) >= 2:
            return _normalize_topic(cleaned, fallback)
    return fallback


def _extract_topic_from_raw(raw: str) -> str:  # 兼容模型偶发返回 fenced JSON 或裸 JSON 的情况。
    cleaned = (raw or "").strip()
    if not cleaned:
        return ""

    if cleaned.startswith("```"):
        cleaned = cleaned.strip("`").strip()
        if cleaned.lower().startswith("json"):
            cleaned = cleaned[4:].strip()

    try:
        data = json.loads(cleaned)
    except Exception:
        return cleaned

    if isinstance(data, dict):
        return str(data.get("topic", "") or "")
    return ""


def _extract_topic_from_result(result: object) -> str:  # 兼容结构化输出与裸文本两种返回形态。
    topic = ""
    if getattr(result, "pydantic", None):
        topic = str(result.pydantic.topic or "")
    if not topic:
        topic = _extract_topic_from_raw(getattr(result, "raw", "") or "")
    return topic


def _read_int_env(name: str, default: int, minimum: int = 1) -> int:  # 环境变量非法时静默回退到默认值，避免启动时炸掉。
    raw = os.getenv(name, "").strip()
    if not raw:
        return default

    try:
        return max(minimum, int(raw))
    except ValueError:
        return default


def get_page_index_max_concurrency() -> int:  # 允许按环境动态调节页索引并发度。
    return _read_int_env(
        "PDF_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY",
        PAGE_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY_DEFAULT,
        minimum=1,
    )


def get_page_index_retry_limit() -> int:  # 允许在不同 OpenRouter 配额/限流环境下快速调重试次数。
    return _read_int_env(
        "PDF_INDEX_RETRY_LIMIT",
        PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_LIMIT_DEFAULT,
        minimum=0,
    )


def _is_retryable_page_index_error(exc: Exception) -> bool:  # 对常见限流、超时、网关波动做谨慎重试。
    error_text = f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}".lower()
    retryable_markers = (
        "429",
        "rate limit",
        "too many requests",
        "timeout",
        "timed out",
        "connection",
        "temporarily unavailable",
        "bad gateway",
        "gateway timeout",
        "service unavailable",
        "502",
        "503",
        "504",
    )
    return any(marker in error_text for marker in retryable_markers)


def build_page_topic_task_prompt(page_number: int, page_text: str, company_name: str = "") -> str:  # 把“单页主题摘要任务”的提示词集中到一处，便于单独调试。
    prompt_parts = [
        "你是一个投行初级分析师，负责给一页 PDF 打一个简短主题标签。",
        "",
        "规则：",
    ]
    prompt_parts.extend(f"- {rule}" for rule in PAGE_INDEX_PROMPT_RULES)
    prompt_parts.extend(
        [
            "",
            f"公司名称：{company_name or PAGE_INDEX_UNKNOWN_COMPANY}",
            f"页码：{page_number}",
            f"当前页文本：{page_text}",
        ]
    )
    return "\n".join(prompt_parts).strip()


# =========================
# Page Index Agent
# =========================

def create_page_indexer_agent() -> Agent:  # 专门负责“逐页读 PDF 并生成短主题”的独立 agent。
    return Agent(
        role=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_ROLE,  # 默认“PDF 逐页索引专员”；可改成更贴近你内部角色定义的名字。
        goal=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_GOAL,  # 默认聚焦“逐页筛页”；可改成更强调招股书目录化摘要。
        backstory=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_BACKSTORY,  # 默认强调“不跨页总结”；可按文档类型微调语境。
        llm=get_llm(
            temperature=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TEMPERATURE,
            timeout=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS,
            max_retries=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_MAX_RETRIES,
        ),  # 逐页预处理要快失败快回退，避免单页卡 10 分钟。
        verbose=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_VERBOSE,  # 默认 True；调试索引过程时保留详细日志。
        allow_delegation=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_ALLOW_DELEGATION,  # 默认 False；逐页摘要任务通常不需要委派。
        reasoning=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_REASONING,  # 默认 False；结构化短任务通常不需要 reasoning。
        cache=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_CACHE,  # 默认 True；相同 prompt 可复用缓存。
        max_retry_limit=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_MAX_RETRIES,
    )

# =========================
# Page Index Task Execution
# =========================

def summarize_page_topic(  # 对单页执行一次摘要任务，输出页码到主题的结构化映射。
    agent: Agent,
    page_number: int,
    page_text: str,
    company_name: str = "",  # 默认空字符串；上游识别出公司名时传入可提升主题稳定性。
) -> PdfPageIndexEntry:
    fallback = PAGE_INDEX_EMPTY_PAGE_TOPIC if not page_text.strip() else f"第{page_number}页"  # 默认空白页用固定标签，非空页则回退为页码标签。
    if not page_text.strip():
        return PdfPageIndexEntry(page_number=page_number, topic=fallback)

    prompt = build_page_topic_task_prompt(page_number=page_number, page_text=page_text, company_name=company_name)  # 先集中生成任务 prompt，方便调试时单独打印。
    started_at = perf_counter()

    try:
        result = agent.kickoff(prompt, response_format=PageTopicSummary)  # 优先用 CrewAI 结构化输出，避免手工猜 JSON。
        topic = _extract_topic_from_result(result)
        elapsed_seconds = perf_counter() - started_at
        print(f"[PDF Index] page {page_number} completed in {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s")
    except Exception as exc:
        elapsed_seconds = perf_counter() - started_at
        print(
            "[PDF Index] page "
            f"{page_number} failed after {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s with "
            f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}"
        )
        topic = _heuristic_topic(page_text, fallback)  # 模型失败时退回启发式标题抽取，保证索引流程不中断。

    return PdfPageIndexEntry(
        page_number=page_number,
        topic=_normalize_topic(str(topic), fallback),
    )


async def summarize_page_topic_async(  # 并发模式下对单页执行异步摘要，和串行版保持同一输出结构。
    page_number: int,
    page_text: str,
    company_name: str,
    total_pages: int,
    semaphore: asyncio.Semaphore,
) -> PdfPageIndexEntry:
    fallback = PAGE_INDEX_EMPTY_PAGE_TOPIC if not page_text.strip() else f"第{page_number}页"
    if not page_text.strip():
        return PdfPageIndexEntry(page_number=page_number, topic=fallback)

    prompt = build_page_topic_task_prompt(
        page_number=page_number,
        page_text=page_text,
        company_name=company_name,
    )
    retry_limit = get_page_index_retry_limit()

    async with semaphore:
        for attempt in range(retry_limit + 1):
            started_at = perf_counter()
            try:
                result = await create_page_indexer_agent().kickoff_async(
                    prompt,
                    response_format=PageTopicSummary,
                )
                topic = _extract_topic_from_result(result)
                elapsed_seconds = perf_counter() - started_at
                print(
                    f"[PDF Index] page {page_number}/{total_pages} "
                    f"completed in {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s"
                )
                return PdfPageIndexEntry(
                    page_number=page_number,
                    topic=_normalize_topic(str(topic), fallback),
                )
            except Exception as exc:
                elapsed_seconds = perf_counter() - started_at
                should_retry = attempt < retry_limit and _is_retryable_page_index_error(exc)
                if should_retry:
                    delay_seconds = PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_BASE_DELAY_SECONDS * (2 ** attempt)
                    print(
                        "[PDF Index] page "
                        f"{page_number}/{total_pages} failed after {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s with "
                        f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}. "
                        f"Retrying in {delay_seconds:.1f}s "
                        f"({attempt + 1}/{retry_limit})"
                    )
                    await asyncio.sleep(delay_seconds)
                    continue

                print(
                    "[PDF Index] page "
                    f"{page_number}/{total_pages} failed after {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s with "
                    f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}"
                )
                topic = _heuristic_topic(page_text, fallback)
                return PdfPageIndexEntry(
                    page_number=page_number,
                    topic=_normalize_topic(str(topic), fallback),
                )

    return PdfPageIndexEntry(page_number=page_number, topic=fallback)


async def summarize_pages_with_bounded_concurrency(  # 用小并发批量索引所有页面，避免一次性打爆 OpenRouter。
    pages: list[str],
    company_name: str = "",
    max_concurrency: int = PAGE_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY_DEFAULT,
) -> list[PdfPageIndexEntry]:
    semaphore = asyncio.Semaphore(max_concurrency)
    total_pages = len(pages)
    tasks = [
        summarize_page_topic_async(
            page_number=page_number,
            page_text=page_text,
            company_name=company_name,
            total_pages=total_pages,
            semaphore=semaphore,
        )
        for page_number, page_text in enumerate(pages, start=1)
    ]
    return await asyncio.gather(*tasks)


# =========================
# Page Index Entrypoint
# =========================

def ensure_pdf_page_index(  # 页索引总入口：优先复用最新 JSON，必要时才重建整本 PDF 的页索引。
    pdf_file_path: str,
    company_name: str = "",  # 默认空字符串；传入公司名可让逐页主题标注更贴近业务语境。
    force_rebuild: bool = PAGE_INDEX_FORCE_REBUILD_DEFAULT,  # 默认 False；改 True 时忽略缓存，强制重建整本索引。
) -> str:
    pdf_path = Path(pdf_file_path).expanduser().resolve()
    if not pdf_path.exists():
        raise FileNotFoundError(f"PDF file does not exist: {pdf_path}")

    index_path = default_page_index_path(pdf_path)  # 固定索引文件名，便于用户和 agent 稳定引用。
    if not force_rebuild and page_index_is_current(pdf_path, index_path):
        set_pdf_context(str(pdf_path), str(index_path))
        return str(index_path)

    pages = extract_pdf_pages(pdf_path)  # 先抽出每一页的纯文本，再逐页做主题标注。
    max_concurrency = get_page_index_max_concurrency()

    if max_concurrency <= 1:
        page_indexer = create_page_indexer_agent()  # 串行模式下复用同一个 agent，减少重复初始化。
        page_entries: list[PdfPageIndexEntry] = []
        for page_number, page_text in enumerate(pages, start=1):
            print(f"[PDF Index] summarizing page {page_number}/{len(pages)}")
            page_entries.append(
                summarize_page_topic(
                    agent=page_indexer,
                    page_number=page_number,
                    page_text=page_text,
                    company_name=company_name,
                )
            )
    else:
        print(
            "[PDF Index] using bounded concurrency "
            f"(max_concurrency={max_concurrency}, pages={len(pages)})"
        )
        page_entries = asyncio.run(
            summarize_pages_with_bounded_concurrency(
                pages=pages,
                company_name=company_name,
                max_concurrency=max_concurrency,
            )
        )

    payload = build_page_index_payload(pdf_path, page_entries)  # 写盘前补齐 PDF 名称、指纹和生成时间等元数据。
    saved_index_path = save_page_index(payload, index_path)  # 把最终页索引 JSON 写入 .cache。
    set_pdf_context(str(pdf_path), saved_index_path)  # 更新共享上下文，让后续工具直接复用这份索引。
    return saved_index_path


# =========================
# Shared Runtime Reset
# =========================

def reset_pdf_preprocessing_runtime_state() -> None:  # 运行前清理共享 PDF 页面工具的内存态，但保留 .cache 磁盘缓存。
    reset_pdf_page_tool_runtime_state()


def reset_pdf_indexing_runtime_state() -> None:  # 兼容旧调用名；实际清理的是预处理阶段共享的 PDF 页面缓存。
    reset_pdf_preprocessing_runtime_state()
```

40	PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_REASONING = False  # 默认 False；该任务短且结构化，通常不需要额外 reasoning。
41	PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_CACHE = True  # 默认 True；相同输入可复用缓存，减少重复调用。
42	PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS = 20  # 逐页短调用不应该无限等到底层默认 600 秒。
43	PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_MAX_RETRIES = 0  # 单页失败直接走启发式兜底，避免一次卡住后再重试。
44	
45	
46	# =========================
47	# Page Index Task Parameters
48	# =========================

50	PAGE_INDEX_TOPIC_MAX_CHARS = 10  # 默认主题最长 10 字；可调大到 12-15 字换取更完整标签。
51	PAGE_INDEX_UNKNOWN_COMPANY = "未知公司"  # 默认公司占位值；上游没识别出公司时用于 prompt。
52	PAGE_INDEX_EMPTY_PAGE_TOPIC = "空白页"  # 默认空白页标签；可改成“扫描页”“图片页”等更贴近团队习惯的词。
53	PAGE_INDEX_FORCE_REBUILD_DEFAULT = False  # 默认优先复用缓存；改成 True 会每次都强制重建索引。
54	PAGE_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY_DEFAULT = 4  # 默认只开小并发，兼顾 OpenRouter 吞吐与稳定性。
55	PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_LIMIT_DEFAULT = 2  # 对 429、超时、网关波动做少量重试，避免瞬时抖动直接退化。
56	PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_BASE_DELAY_SECONDS = 2.0  # 并发场景下使用指数退避，给上游路由与限流一点缓冲时间。
57	PAGE_INDEX_PROMPT_RULES = (  # 默认任务规则；可逐条增删来调整主题标签风格。
58	    "只输出一个 `topic` 字段。",
59	    f"`topic` 最多 {PAGE_INDEX_TOPIC_MAX_CHARS} 个字。",
60	    "只关注当前这一页，不要总结整份文档。",
61	    "尽量使用具体的业务主题，不要使用空泛表述。",
62	    "如果本页主要是表格，就概括表格的主题。",
63	    "如果本页难以判断，就返回一个谨慎、简短的主题。",
64	    "不要输出解释、前后缀、Markdown 代码块或额外文本。",
65	)
66	
67	# =========================
68	# Page Index Models
69	# =========================
70	
71	class PageTopicSummary(BaseModel):
72	    topic: str = Field(..., description="当前页的简短主题标签")  # 单页主题字段，供后续 agent 快速筛页。
73	
74	
75	# =========================
76	# Page Index Helpers
77	# =========================
78	
79	def _normalize_topic(topic: str, fallback: str) -> str:  # 清洗 LLM 或启发式产出的主题，统一成稳定短标签。
80	    normalized = " ".join((topic or "").split())
81	    normalized = normalized.replace('"', "").replace("'", "").replace("`", "").strip(" ,.;:()[]{}")
82	    compact = normalized.replace(" ", "").lower()
83	    if compact in {"json", "{", "}", "topic", "none", "null"}:
84	        normalized = ""
85	    if not normalized:
86	        normalized = fallback
87	    return normalized[:PAGE_INDEX_TOPIC_MAX_CHARS]
88	
89	
90	def _heuristic_topic(page_text: str, fallback: str) -> str:  # LLM 失败时退化为“取首个像标题的文本”。
91	    for line in page_text.splitlines():
92	        cleaned = " ".join(line.split()).strip(" ,.;:()[]{}")
93	        if len(cleaned) >= 2:
94	            return _normalize_topic(cleaned, fallback)
95	    return fallback
96	
97	
98	def _extract_topic_from_raw(raw: str) -> str:  # 兼容模型偶发返回 fenced JSON 或裸 JSON 的情况。
99	    cleaned = (raw or "").strip()
100	    if not cleaned:
101	        return ""
102	
103	    if cleaned.startswith("```"):
104	        cleaned = cleaned.strip("`").strip()
105	        if cleaned.lower().startswith("json"):
106	            cleaned = cleaned[4:].strip()
107	
108	    try:
109	        data = json.loads(cleaned)
110	    except Exception:
111	        return cleaned
112	
113	    if isinstance(data, dict):
114	        return str(data.get("topic", "") or "")
115	    return ""
116	
117	
118	def _extract_topic_from_result(result: object) -> str:  # 兼容结构化输出与裸文本两种返回形态。
119	    topic = ""
120	    if getattr(result, "pydantic", None):
121	        topic = str(result.pydantic.topic or "")
122	    if not topic:
123	        topic = _extract_topic_from_raw(getattr(result, "raw", "") or "")
124	    return topic
125	
126	
127	def _read_int_env(name: str, default: int, minimum: int = 1) -> int:  # 环境变量非法时静默回退到默认值，避免启动时炸掉。
128	    raw = os.getenv(name, "").strip()
129	    if not raw:
130	        return default
131	
132	    try:
133	        return max(minimum, int(raw))
134	    except ValueError:
135	        return default
136	
137	
138	def get_page_index_max_concurrency() -> int:  # 允许按环境动态调节页索引并发度。
139	    return _read_int_env(
140	        "PDF_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY",
141	        PAGE_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY_DEFAULT,
142	        minimum=1,
143	    )
144	
145	
146	def get_page_index_retry_limit() -> int:  # 允许在不同 OpenRouter 配额/限流环境下快速调重试次数。
147	    return _read_int_env(
148	        "PDF_INDEX_RETRY_LIMIT",
149	        PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_LIMIT_DEFAULT,
150	        minimum=0,
151	    )
152	
153	
154	def _is_retryable_page_index_error(exc: Exception) -> bool:  # 对常见限流、超时、网关波动做谨慎重试。
155	    error_text = f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}".lower()
156	    retryable_markers = (
157	        "429",
158	        "rate limit",
159	        "too many requests",
160	        "timeout",
161	        "timed out",
162	        "connection",
163	        "temporarily unavailable",
164	        "bad gateway",
165	        "gateway timeout",
166	        "service unavailable",
167	        "502",
168	        "503",
169	        "504",
170	    )
171	    return any(marker in error_text for marker in retryable_markers)
172	
173	
174	def build_page_topic_task_prompt(page_number: int, page_text: str, company_name: str = "") -> str:  # 把“单页主题摘要任务”的提示词集中到一处，便于单独调试。
175	    prompt_parts = [
176	        "你是一个投行初级分析师，负责给一页 PDF 打一个简短主题标签。",
177	        "",
178	        "规则：",
179	    ]
180	    prompt_parts.extend(f"- {rule}" for rule in PAGE_INDEX_PROMPT_RULES)
181	    prompt_parts.extend(
182	        [
183	            "",
184	            f"公司名称：{company_name or PAGE_INDEX_UNKNOWN_COMPANY}",
185	            f"页码：{page_number}",
186	            f"当前页文本：{page_text}",
187	        ]
188	    )
189	    return "\n".join(prompt_parts).strip()
190	
191	
192	# =========================
193	# Page Index Agent
194	# =========================
195	
196	def create_page_indexer_agent() -> Agent:  # 专门负责“逐页读 PDF 并生成短主题”的独立 agent。
197	    return Agent(
198	        role=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_ROLE,  # 默认“PDF 逐页索引专员”；可改成更贴近你内部角色定义的名字。
199	        goal=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_GOAL,  # 默认聚焦“逐页筛页”；可改成更强调招股书目录化摘要。
200	        backstory=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_BACKSTORY,  # 默认强调“不跨页总结”；可按文档类型微调语境。
201	        llm=get_llm(
202	            temperature=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TEMPERATURE,
203	            timeout=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS,
204	            max_retries=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_MAX_RETRIES,
205	        ),  # 逐页预处理要快失败快回退，避免单页卡 10 分钟。
206	        verbose=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_VERBOSE,  # 默认 True；调试索引过程时保留详细日志。
207	        allow_delegation=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_ALLOW_DELEGATION,  # 默认 False；逐页摘要任务通常不需要委派。
208	        reasoning=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_REASONING,  # 默认 False；结构化短任务通常不需要 reasoning。
209	        cache=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_CACHE,  # 默认 True；相同 prompt 可复用缓存。
210	        max_retry_limit=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_MAX_RETRIES,
211	    )
212	
213	# =========================
214	# Page Index Task Execution
215	# =========================
216	
217	def summarize_page_topic(  # 对单页执行一次摘要任务，输出页码到主题的结构化映射。
218	    agent: Agent,
219	    page_number: int,
220	    page_text: str,
221	    company_name: str = "",  # 默认空字符串；上游识别出公司名时传入可提升主题稳定性。
222	) -> PdfPageIndexEntry:
223	    fallback = PAGE_INDEX_EMPTY_PAGE_TOPIC if not page_text.strip() else f"第{page_number}页"  # 默认空白页用固定标签，非空页则回退为页码标签。
224	    if not page_text.strip():
225	        return PdfPageIndexEntry(page_number=page_number, topic=fallback)
226	
227	    prompt = build_page_topic_task_prompt(page_number=page_number, page_text=page_text, company_name=company_name)  # 先集中生成任务 prompt，方便调试时单独打印。
228	    started_at = perf_counter()
229	
230	    try:
231	        result = agent.kickoff(prompt, response_format=PageTopicSummary)  # 优先用 CrewAI 结构化输出，避免手工猜 JSON。
232	        topic = _extract_topic_from_result(result)
233	        elapsed_seconds = perf_counter() - started_at
234	        print(f"[PDF Index] page {page_number} completed in {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s")
235	    except Exception as exc:
236	        elapsed_seconds = perf_counter() - started_at
237	        print(
238	            "[PDF Index] page "
239	            f"{page_number} failed after {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s with "
240	            f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}"
241	        )
242	        topic = _heuristic_topic(page_text, fallback)  # 模型失败时退回启发式标题抽取，保证索引流程不中断。
243	
244	    return PdfPageIndexEntry(
245	        page_number=page_number,
246	        topic=_normalize_topic(str(topic), fallback),
247	    )
248	
249	
250	async def summarize_page_topic_async(  # 并发模式下对单页执行异步摘要，和串行版保持同一输出结构。
251	    page_number: int,
252	    page_text: str,
253	    company_name: str,
254	    total_pages: int,
255	    semaphore: asyncio.Semaphore,
256	) -> PdfPageIndexEntry:
257	    fallback = PAGE_INDEX_EMPTY_PAGE_TOPIC if not page_text.strip() else f"第{page_number}页"
258	    if not page_text.strip():
259	        return PdfPageIndexEntry(page_number=page_number, topic=fallback)
260
```

315	async def summarize_pages_with_bounded_concurrency(  # 用小并发批量索引所有页面，避免一次性打爆 OpenRouter。
316	    pages: list[str],
317	    company_name: str = "",
318	    max_concurrency: int = PAGE_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY_DEFAULT,
319	) -> list[PdfPageIndexEntry]:
320	    semaphore = asyncio.Semaphore(max_concurrency)
321	    total_pages = len(pages)
322	    tasks = [
323	        summarize_page_topic_async(
324	            page_number=page_number,
325	            page_text=page_text,
326	            company_name=company_name,
327	            total_pages=total_pages,
328	            semaphore=semaphore,
329	        )
330	        for page_number, page_text in enumerate(pages, start=1)
331	    ]
332	    return await asyncio.gather(*tasks)
333	
334	
335	# =========================
336	# Page Index Entrypoint
337	# =========================
338	
339	def ensure_pdf_page_index(  # 页索引总入口：优先复用最新 JSON，必要时才重建整本 PDF 的页索引。
340	    pdf_file_path: str,
341	    company_name: str = "",  # 默认空字符串；传入公司名可让逐页主题标注更贴近业务语境。
342	    force_rebuild: bool = PAGE_INDEX_FORCE_REBUILD_DEFAULT,  # 默认 False；改 True 时忽略缓存，强制重建整本索引。
343	) -> str:
344	    pdf_path = Path(pdf_file_path).expanduser().resolve()
345	    if not pdf_path.exists():
346	        raise FileNotFoundError(f"PDF file does not exist: {pdf_path}")
347	
348	    index_path = default_page_index_path(pdf_path)  # 固定索引文件名，便于用户和 agent 稳定引用。
349	    if not force_rebuild and page_index_is_current(pdf_path, index_path):
350	        set_pdf_context(str(pdf_path), str(index_path))
351	        return str(index_path)
352	
353	    pages = extract_pdf_pages(pdf_path)  # 先抽出每一页的纯文本，再逐页做主题标注。
354	    max_concurrency = get_page_index_max_concurrency()
355	
356	    if max_concurrency <= 1:
357	        page_indexer = create_page_indexer_agent()  # 串行模式下复用同一个 agent，减少重复初始化。
358	        page_entries: list[PdfPageIndexEntry] = []
359	        for page_number, page_text in enumerate(pages, start=1):
360	            print(f"[PDF Index] summarizing page {page_number}/{len(pages)}")
361	            page_entries.append(
362	                summarize_page_topic(
363	                    agent=page_indexer,
364	                    page_number=page_number,
365	                    page_text=page_text,
366	                    company_name=company_name,
367	                )
368	            )
369	    else:
370	        print(
371	            "[PDF Index] using bounded concurrency "
372	            f"(max_concurrency={max_concurrency}, pages={len(pages)})"
373	        )
374	        page_entries = asyncio.run(
375	            summarize_pages_with_bounded_concurrency(
376	                pages=pages,
377	                company_name=company_name,
378	                max_concurrency=max_concurrency,
379	            )
380	        )
381	
382	    payload = build_page_index_payload(pdf_path, page_entries)  # 写盘前补齐 PDF 名称、指纹和生成时间等元数据。
383	    saved_index_path = save_page_index(payload, index_path)  # 把最终页索引 JSON 写入 .cache。
384	    set_pdf_context(str(pdf_path), saved_index_path)  # 更新共享上下文，让后续工具直接复用这份索引。
385	    return saved_index_path

### 0083 ASSISTANT (final_answer)

```text
可以，而且我已经把它改成“有上限的并发索引”了。核心改动都在 [pdf_indexing.py:54](C:/PyProjects/automated_research_report_generator_v0.1/src/automated_research_report_generator_v0_1/pdf_indexing.py#L54)、[pdf_indexing.py:250](C:/PyProjects/automated_research_report_generator_v0.1/src/automated_research_report_generator_v0_1/pdf_indexing.py#L250) 和 [pdf_indexing.py:339](C:/PyProjects/automated_research_report_generator_v0.1/src/automated_research_report_generator_v0_1/pdf_indexing.py#L339)。现在不再是单纯 `for page in pages -> kickoff()` 串行跑，而是用 `kickoff_async + asyncio.Semaphore` 做有界并发；默认并发度是 `4`，并且加了 429/超时/网关波动的退避重试，失败时仍保留你原来的启发式兜底。

结合 OpenRouter 的官方说明，这样做是合理的：免费模型有明确的 20 RPM / 每日额度限制，而付费账号没有统一的平台级硬限，但容量是“全局治理”的，而且不同模型会有不同限制，所以最稳的方式不是无脑全开，而是这种小并发、可回退的策略。OpenRouter 也支持 `:nitro` / throughput routing，如果你后面想把页索引再提速，可以考虑把索引专用模型切成吞吐优先路由。你的本地 CrewAI 是 `1.12.2`，我也确认了 `Agent.kickoff_async` 在这个版本里可用。

现在你可以直接通过环境变量调：
- `PDF_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY=4`
- `PDF_INDEX_RETRY_LIMIT=2`

建议先从 `4` 开始，如果你的 OpenRouter 账号是稳定付费额度，可以试 `6`；如果出现 429 或明显抖动，再退回 `3-4`。我做了语法检查和运行时 API 可用性检查，但没有做真实联网压测，因为当前环境网络受限。

参考：
[CrewAI Changelog](https://docs.crewai.com/en/changelog)  
[CrewAI LLM Docs](https://docs.crewai.com/en/concepts/llms)  
[OpenRouter Limits](https://openrouter.ai/docs/api-reference/limits/)  
[OpenRouter FAQ](https://openrouter.ai/docs/faq)  
[OpenRouter Provider Routing / Nitro](https://openrouter.ai/docs/guides/routing/provider-selection)

如果你愿意，我下一步可以继续帮你做两件事里的一个：
1. 给这个并发索引加一个小 benchmark 日志，方便你看串行 vs 并发提升了多少。
2. 再把索引 prompt 做成“按页截断文本 + 吞吐优先模型”，进一步压缩成本和延迟。
```

# =========================
# Page Index Agent Parameters
# =========================

PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_ROLE = "PDF 逐页索引专员"  # 默认角色名；可改成更贴近你内部分工的中文称呼。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_GOAL = (  # 默认目标；可改成更强调“筛页”或“目录化索引”的版本。
    "逐页读取 PDF，并为每一页生成一个简短主题标签，帮助后续 agent 快速判断哪些页与自己的分析任务相关。"
)
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_BACKSTORY = (  # 默认背景设定；可改成更偏招股书、年报或行业报告场景。
    "你专门负责按页阅读 PDF。你不会跨页总结，也不会提前做整份文档分析。"
    "你的唯一职责是只根据当前这一页的内容，输出一个非常短、便于筛页的主题标签。"
)
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TEMPERATURE = 0.1  # 默认 0.1；可改到 0 更稳，0.2-0.3 会更灵活但更易漂移。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_VERBOSE = True  # 默认 True；调试时方便看 agent 过程，可改 False 收敛日志。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_ALLOW_DELEGATION = False  # 默认 False；该 agent 只做单页索引，不需要委派。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_REASONING = False  # 默认 False；该任务短且结构化，通常不需要额外 reasoning。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_CACHE = True  # 默认 True；相同输入可复用缓存，减少重复调用。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS = 20  # 逐页短调用不应该无限等到底层默认 600 秒。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_MAX_RETRIES = 0  # 单页失败直接走启发式兜底，避免一次卡住后再重试。


# =========================
# Page Index Task Parameters
# =========================

PAGE_INDEX_TOPIC_MAX_CHARS = 10  # 默认主题最长 10 字；可调大到 12-15 字换取更完整标签。
PAGE_INDEX_UNKNOWN_COMPANY = "未知公司"  # 默认公司占位值；上游没识别出公司时用于 prompt。
PAGE_INDEX_EMPTY_PAGE_TOPIC = "空白页"  # 默认空白页标签；可改成“扫描页”“图片页”等更贴近团队习惯的词。
PAGE_INDEX_FORCE_REBUILD_DEFAULT = False  # 默认优先复用缓存；改成 True 会每次都强制重建索引。
PAGE_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY_DEFAULT = 4  # 默认只开小并发，兼顾 OpenRouter 吞吐与稳定性。
PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_LIMIT_DEFAULT = 2  # 对 429、超时、网关波动做少量重试，避免瞬时抖动直接退化。
PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_BASE_DELAY_SECONDS = 2.0  # 并发场景下使用指数退避，给上游路由与限流一点缓冲时间。
PAGE_INDEX_PROMPT_RULES = (  # 默认任务规则；可逐条增删来调整主题标签风格。
    "只输出一个 `topic` 字段。",
    f"`topic` 最多 {PAGE_INDEX_TOPIC_MAX_CHARS} 个字。",
    "只关注当前这一页，不要总结整份文档。",
    "尽量使用具体的业务主题，不要使用空泛表述。",
    "如果本页主要是表格，就概括表格的主题。",
    "如果本页难以判断，就返回一个谨慎、简短的主题。",
    "不要输出解释、前后缀、Markdown 代码块或额外文本。",
)

# =========================
# Page Index Models
# =========================

class PageTopicSummary(BaseModel):
    topic: str = Field(..., description="当前页的简短主题标签")  # 单页主题字段，供后续 agent 快速筛页。


# =========================
# Page Index Helpers
# =========================

def _normalize_topic(topic: str, fallback: str) -> str:  # 清洗 LLM 或启发式产出的主题，统一成稳定短标签。
    normalized = " ".join((topic or "").split())

import contextvars
import threading
from typing import Any
import urllib.request
import warnings

from crewai.agent.core import Agent
from crewai.agent.planning_config import PlanningConfig
from crewai.crew import Crew
from crewai.crews.crew_output import CrewOutput
from crewai.flow.flow import Flow
from crewai.knowledge.knowledge import Knowledge
from crewai.llm import LLM
from crewai.llms.base_llm import BaseLLM
from crewai.process import Process
from crewai.task import Task
from crewai.tasks.llm_guardrail import LLMGuardrail
from crewai.tasks.task_output import TaskOutput
from crewai.telemetry.telemetry import Telemetry


def _suppress_pydantic_deprecation_warnings() -> None:
    """Suppress Pydantic deprecation warnings using targeted monkey patch."""
    original_warn = warnings.warn

    def filtered_warn(
        message: Any,
        category: type | None = None,
        stacklevel: int = 1,
        source: Any = None,
    ) -> Any:
        if (
            category
            and hasattr(category, "__module__")
            and category.__module__ == "pydantic.warnings"
        ):
            return None
        return original_warn(message, category, stacklevel + 1, source)

    warnings.warn = filtered_warn  # type: ignore[assignment]


_suppress_pydantic_deprecation_warnings()

__version__ = "1.12.2"
_telemetry_submitted = False


def _track_install() -> None:
    """Track package installation/first-use via Scarf analytics."""
    global _telemetry_submitted

    if _telemetry_submitted or Telemetry._is_telemetry_disabled():
        return

    try:
        pixel_url = "https://api.scarf.sh/v2/packages/CrewAI/crewai/docs/00f2dad1-8334-4a39-934e-003b2e1146db"

        req = urllib.request.Request(pixel_url)  # noqa: S310
        req.add_header("User-Agent", f"CrewAI-Python/{__version__}")

        with urllib.request.urlopen(req, timeout=2):  # noqa: S310
            _telemetry_submitted = True
    except Exception:  # noqa: S110
        pass


def _track_install_async() -> None:
    """Track installation in background thread to avoid blocking imports."""
    if not Telemetry._is_telemetry_disabled():
        ctx = contextvars.copy_context()
        thread = threading.Thread(target=ctx.run, args=(_track_install,), daemon=True)
        thread.start()


_track_install_async()

_LAZY_IMPORTS: dict[str, tuple[str, str]] = {
    "Memory": ("crewai.memory.unified_memory", "Memory"),
}


def __getattr__(name: str) -> Any:
    """Lazily import heavy modules (e.g. Memory 鈫?lancedb) on first access."""
    if name in _LAZY_IMPORTS:
        module_path, attr = _LAZY_IMPORTS[name]
        import importlib

        mod = importlib.import_module(module_path)
        val = getattr(mod, attr)
        globals()[name] = val
        return val
    raise AttributeError(f"module 'crewai' has no attribute {name!r}")

# =========================
# Page Index Agent Parameters
# =========================

PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_ROLE = "PDF 逐页索引专员"  # 默认角色名；可改成更贴近你内部分工的中文称呼。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_GOAL = (  # 默认目标；可改成更强调“筛页”或“目录化索引”的版本。
    "逐页读取 PDF，并为每一页生成一个简短主题标签，帮助后续 agent 快速判断哪些页与自己的分析任务相关。"
)
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_BACKSTORY = (  # 默认背景设定；可改成更偏招股书、年报或行业报告场景。
    "你专门负责按页阅读 PDF。你不会跨页总结，也不会提前做整份文档分析。"
    "你的唯一职责是只根据当前这一页的内容，输出一个非常短、便于筛页的主题标签。"
)
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TEMPERATURE = 0.1  # 默认 0.1；可改到 0 更稳，0.2-0.3 会更灵活但更易漂移。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_VERBOSE = True  # 默认 True；调试时方便看 agent 过程，可改 False 收敛日志。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_ALLOW_DELEGATION = False  # 默认 False；该 agent 只做单页索引，不需要委派。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_REASONING = False  # 默认 False；该任务短且结构化，通常不需要额外 reasoning。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_CACHE = True  # 默认 True；相同输入可复用缓存，减少重复调用。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS = 20  # 逐页短调用不应该无限等到底层默认 600 秒。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_MAX_RETRIES = 0  # 单页失败直接走启发式兜底，避免一次卡住后再重试。


# =========================
# Page Index Task Parameters
# =========================

PAGE_INDEX_TOPIC_MAX_CHARS = 10  # 默认主题最长 10 字；可调大到 12-15 字换取更完整标签。
PAGE_INDEX_UNKNOWN_COMPANY = "未知公司"  # 默认公司占位值；上游没识别出公司时用于 prompt。
PAGE_INDEX_EMPTY_PAGE_TOPIC = "空白页"  # 默认空白页标签；可改成“扫描页”“图片页”等更贴近团队习惯的词。
PAGE_INDEX_FORCE_REBUILD_DEFAULT = False  # 默认优先复用缓存；改成 True 会每次都强制重建索引。
PAGE_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY_DEFAULT = 4  # 默认只开小并发，兼顾 OpenRouter 吞吐与稳定性。
PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_LIMIT_DEFAULT = 2  # 对 429、超时、网关波动做少量重试，避免瞬时抖动直接退化。
PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_BASE_DELAY_SECONDS = 2.0  # 并发场景下使用指数退避，给上游路由与限流一点缓冲时间。

    "只输出一个 `topic` 字段。",
    f"`topic` 最多 {PAGE_INDEX_TOPIC_MAX_CHARS} 个字。",
    "只关注当前这一页，不要总结整份文档。",
    "尽量使用具体的业务主题，不要使用空泛表述。",
    "如果本页主要是表格，就概括表格的主题。",
    "如果本页难以判断，就返回一个谨慎、简短的主题。",
    "不要输出解释、前后缀、Markdown 代码块或额外文本。",
)

# =========================
# Page Index Models
# =========================

class PageTopicSummary(BaseModel):
    topic: str = Field(..., description="当前页的简短主题标签")  # 单页主题字段，供后续 agent 快速筛页。


# =========================
# Page Index Helpers
# =========================

def _normalize_topic(topic: str, fallback: str) -> str:  # 清洗 LLM 或启发式产出的主题，统一成稳定短标签。
    normalized = " ".join((topic or "").split())
    normalized = normalized.replace('"', "").replace("'", "").replace("`", "").strip(" ,.;:()[]{}")
    compact = normalized.replace(" ", "").lower()
    if compact in {"json", "{", "}", "topic", "none", "null"}:
        normalized = ""
    if not normalized:
        normalized = fallback
    return normalized[:PAGE_INDEX_TOPIC_MAX_CHARS]


def _heuristic_topic(page_text: str, fallback: str) -> str:  # LLM 失败时退化为“取首个像标题的文本”。
    for line in page_text.splitlines():
        cleaned = " ".join(line.split()).strip(" ,.;:()[]{}")
        if len(cleaned) >= 2:
            return _normalize_topic(cleaned, fallback)
    return fallback


def _extract_topic_from_raw(raw: str) -> str:  # 兼容模型偶发返回 fenced JSON 或裸 JSON 的情况。
    cleaned = (raw or "").strip()
    if not cleaned:
        return ""

    if cleaned.startswith("```"):
        cleaned = cleaned.strip("`").strip()
        if cleaned.lower().startswith("json"):
            cleaned = cleaned[4:].strip()

    try:
        data = json.loads(cleaned)
    except Exception:
        return cleaned

    if isinstance(data, dict):
        return str(data.get("topic", "") or "")
    return ""


def _extract_topic_from_result(result: object) -> str:  # 兼容结构化输出与裸文本两种返回形态。
    topic = ""
    if getattr(result, "pydantic", None):
        topic = str(result.pydantic.topic or "")
    if not topic:
        topic = _extract_topic_from_raw(getattr(result, "raw", "") or "")
    return topic


def _read_int_env(name: str, default: int, minimum: int = 1) -> int:  # 环境变量非法时静默回退到默认值，避免启动时炸掉。
    raw = os.getenv(name, "").strip()
    if not raw:
        return default

    try:
        return max(minimum, int(raw))
    except ValueError:
        return default


def get_page_index_max_concurrency() -> int:  # 允许按环境动态调节页索引并发度。
    return _read_int_env(
        "PDF_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY",
        PAGE_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY_DEFAULT,
        minimum=1,
    )


def get_page_index_retry_limit() -> int:  # 允许在不同 OpenRouter 配额/限流环境下快速调重试次数。
    return _read_int_env(
        "PDF_INDEX_RETRY_LIMIT",
        PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_LIMIT_DEFAULT,
        minimum=0,
    )


def _is_retryable_page_index_error(exc: Exception) -> bool:  # 对常见限流、超时、网关波动做谨慎重试。
    error_text = f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}".lower()
    retryable_markers = (
        "429",
        "rate limit",
        "too many requests",
        "timeout",
        "timed out",
        "connection",
        "temporarily unavailable",
        "bad gateway",
        "gateway timeout",
        "service unavailable",
        "502",
        "503",
        "504",
    )
    return any(marker in error_text for marker in retryable_markers)


def build_page_topic_task_prompt(page_number: int, page_text: str, company_name: str = "") -> str:  # 把“单页主题摘要任务”的提示词集中到一处，便于单独调试。
    prompt_parts = [
        "你是一个投行初级分析师，负责给一页 PDF 打一个简短主题标签。",
        "",
        "规则：",
    ]
    prompt_parts.extend(f"- {rule}" for rule in PAGE_INDEX_PROMPT_RULES)
    prompt_parts.extend(
        [
            "",
            f"公司名称：{company_name or PAGE_INDEX_UNKNOWN_COMPANY}",
            f"页码：{page_number}",
            f"当前页文本：{page_text}",
        ]
    )
    return "\n".join(prompt_parts).strip()


# =========================
# Page Index Agent
# =========================

def create_page_indexer_agent() -> Agent:  # 专门负责“逐页读 PDF 并生成短主题”的独立 agent。
    return Agent(
        role=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_ROLE,  # 默认“PDF 逐页索引专员”；可改成更贴近你内部角色定义的名字。
        goal=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_GOAL,  # 默认聚焦“逐页筛页”；可改成更强调招股书目录化摘要。
        backstory=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_BACKSTORY,  # 默认强调“不跨页总结”；可按文档类型微调语境。
        llm=get_llm(
            temperature=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TEMPERATURE,
            timeout=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS,
            max_retries=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_MAX_RETRIES,
        ),  # 逐页预处理要快失败快回退，避免单页卡 10 分钟。
        verbose=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_VERBOSE,  # 默认 True；调试索引过程时保留详细日志。
        allow_delegation=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_ALLOW_DELEGATION,  # 默认 False；逐页摘要任务通常不需要委派。
        reasoning=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_REASONING,  # 默认 False；结构化短任务通常不需要 reasoning。
        cache=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_CACHE,  # 默认 True；相同 prompt 可复用缓存。
        max_retry_limit=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_MAX_RETRIES,
    )

# =========================
# Page Index Task Execution
# =========================

def summarize_page_topic(  # 对单页执行一次摘要任务，输出页码到主题的结构化映射。
    agent: Agent,
    page_number: int,
    page_text: str,
    company_name: str = "",  # 默认空字符串；上游识别出公司名时传入可提升主题稳定性。
) -> PdfPageIndexEntry:
    fallback = PAGE_INDEX_EMPTY_PAGE_TOPIC if not page_text.strip() else f"第{page_number}页"  # 默认空白页用固定标签，非空页则回退为页码标签。
    if not page_text.strip():
        return PdfPageIndexEntry(page_number=page_number, topic=fallback)

    prompt = build_page_topic_task_prompt(page_number=page_number, page_text=page_text, company_name=company_name)  # 先集中生成任务 prompt，方便调试时单独打印。
    started_at = perf_counter()

    try:
        result = agent.kickoff(prompt, response_format=PageTopicSummary)  # 优先用 CrewAI 结构化输出，避免手工猜 JSON。
        topic = _extract_topic_from_result(result)
        elapsed_seconds = perf_counter() - started_at
        print(f"[PDF Index] page {page_number} completed in {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s")
    except Exception as exc:
        elapsed_seconds = perf_counter() - started_at
        print(
            "[PDF Index] page "
            f"{page_number} failed after {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s with "
            f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}"
        )
        topic = _heuristic_topic(page_text, fallback)  # 模型失败时退回启发式标题抽取，保证索引流程不中断。

    return PdfPageIndexEntry(
        page_number=page_number,
        topic=_normalize_topic(str(topic), fallback),
    )


async def summarize_page_topic_async(  # 并发模式下对单页执行异步摘要，和串行版保持同一输出结构。
    page_number: int,
    page_text: str,
    company_name: str,
    total_pages: int,
    semaphore: asyncio.Semaphore,
) -> PdfPageIndexEntry:
    fallback = PAGE_INDEX_EMPTY_PAGE_TOPIC if not page_text.strip() else f"第{page_number}页"
    if not page_text.strip():
        return PdfPageIndexEntry(page_number=page_number, topic=fallback)

    prompt = build_page_topic_task_prompt(
        page_number=page_number,
        page_text=page_text,
        company_name=company_name,
    )
    retry_limit = get_page_index_retry_limit()

    async with semaphore:
        for attempt in range(retry_limit + 1):
            started_at = perf_counter()
            try:
                result = await create_page_indexer_agent().kickoff_async(
                    prompt,
                    response_format=PageTopicSummary,
                )
                topic = _extract_topic_from_result(result)
                elapsed_seconds = perf_counter() - started_at
                print(
                    f"[PDF Index] page {page_number}/{total_pages} "
                    f"completed in {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s"
                )
                return PdfPageIndexEntry(
                    page_number=page_number,
                    topic=_normalize_topic(str(topic), fallback),
                )
            except Exception as exc:
                elapsed_seconds = perf_counter() - started_at
                should_retry = attempt < retry_limit and _is_retryable_page_index_error(exc)
                if should_retry:
                    delay_seconds = PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_BASE_DELAY_SECONDS * (2 ** attempt)
                    print(
                        "[PDF Index] page "
                        f"{page_number}/{total_pages} failed after {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s with "
                        f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}. "
                        f"Retrying in {delay_seconds:.1f}s "
                        f"({attempt + 1}/{retry_limit})"
                    )
                    await asyncio.sleep(delay_seconds)
                    continue

                print(
                    "[PDF Index] page "
                    f"{page_number}/{total_pages} failed after {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s with "
                    f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}"
                )
                topic = _heuristic_topic(page_text, fallback)
                return PdfPageIndexEntry(
                    page_number=page_number,
                    topic=_normalize_topic(str(topic), fallback),
                )

    return PdfPageIndexEntry(page_number=page_number, topic=fallback)


async def summarize_pages_with_bounded_concurrency(  # 用小并发批量索引所有页面，避免一次性打爆 OpenRouter。
    pages: list[str],
    company_name: str = "",
    max_concurrency: int = PAGE_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY_DEFAULT,
) -> list[PdfPageIndexEntry]:
    semaphore = asyncio.Semaphore(max_concurrency)
    total_pages = len(pages)
    tasks = [
        summarize_page_topic_async(
            page_number=page_number,
            page_text=page_text,
            company_name=company_name,
            total_pages=total_pages,
            semaphore=semaphore,
        )
        for page_number, page_text in enumerate(pages, start=1)
    ]
    return await asyncio.gather(*tasks)


# =========================
# Page Index Entrypoint
# =========================

def ensure_pdf_page_index(  # 页索引总入口：优先复用最新 JSON，必要时才重建整本 PDF 的页索引。
    pdf_file_path: str,
    company_name: str = "",  # 默认空字符串；传入公司名可让逐页主题标注更贴近业务语境。
    force_rebuild: bool = PAGE_INDEX_FORCE_REBUILD_DEFAULT,  # 默认 False；改 True 时忽略缓存，强制重建整本索引。
) -> str:
    pdf_path = Path(pdf_file_path).expanduser().resolve()
    if not pdf_path.exists():
        raise FileNotFoundError(f"PDF file does not exist: {pdf_path}")

    index_path = default_page_index_path(pdf_path)  # 固定索引文件名，便于用户和 agent 稳定引用。
    if not force_rebuild and page_index_is_current(pdf_path, index_path):
        set_pdf_context(str(pdf_path), str(index_path))
        return str(index_path)

    pages = extract_pdf_pages(pdf_path)  # 先抽出每一页的纯文本，再逐页做主题标注。
    max_concurrency = get_page_index_max_concurrency()

    if max_concurrency <= 1:
        page_indexer = create_page_indexer_agent()  # 串行模式下复用同一个 agent，减少重复初始化。
        page_entries: list[PdfPageIndexEntry] = []
        for page_number, page_text in enumerate(pages, start=1):
            print(f"[PDF Index] summarizing page {page_number}/{len(pages)}")
            page_entries.append(
                summarize_page_topic(
                    agent=page_indexer,
                    page_number=page_number,
                    page_text=page_text,
                    company_name=company_name,
                )
            )
    else:
        print(
            "[PDF Index] using bounded concurrency "
            f"(max_concurrency={max_concurrency}, pages={len(pages)})"
        )
        page_entries = asyncio.run(
            summarize_pages_with_bounded_concurrency(
                pages=pages,
                company_name=company_name,
                max_concurrency=max_concurrency,
            )
        )

    payload = build_page_index_payload(pdf_path, page_entries)  # 写盘前补齐 PDF 名称、指纹和生成时间等元数据。
    saved_index_path = save_page_index(payload, index_path)  # 把最终页索引 JSON 写入 .cache。
    set_pdf_context(str(pdf_path), saved_index_path)  # 更新共享上下文，让后续工具直接复用这份索引。
    return saved_index_path


# =========================
# Shared Runtime Reset
# =========================

def reset_pdf_preprocessing_runtime_state() -> None:  # 运行前清理共享 PDF 页面工具的内存态，但保留 .cache 磁盘缓存。
    reset_pdf_page_tool_runtime_state()


def reset_pdf_indexing_runtime_state() -> None:  # 兼容旧调用名；实际清理的是预处理阶段共享的 PDF 页面缓存。
    reset_pdf_preprocessing_runtime_state()
```

def _kickoff_with_a2a_support(
    agent: LiteAgent,
    original_kickoff: Callable[..., LiteAgentOutput],
    messages: str | list[LLMMessage],
    response_format: type[BaseModel] | None,
    input_files: dict[str, FileInput] | None,
    extension_registry: Any,
) -> LiteAgentOutput:
    """Wrap kickoff with A2A delegation using Task adapter.

    Args:
        agent: The LiteAgent instance.
        original_kickoff: The original kickoff method.
        messages: Input messages.
        response_format: Optional response format.
        input_files: Optional input files.
        extension_registry: A2A extension registry.

    Returns:
        LiteAgentOutput from either local execution or A2A delegation.
    """
    from crewai.a2a.utils.response_model import get_a2a_agents_and_response_model
    from crewai.a2a.wrapper import _execute_task_with_a2a
    from crewai.task import Task

    a2a_agents, agent_response_model = get_a2a_agents_and_response_model(agent.a2a)

    if not a2a_agents:
        return original_kickoff(messages, response_format, input_files)

    if isinstance(messages, str):
        description = messages
    else:
        content = next(
            (m["content"] for m in reversed(messages) if m["role"] == "user"),
            None,
        )
        description = content if isinstance(content, str) else ""

    if not description:
        return original_kickoff(messages, response_format, input_files)

    fake_task = Task(
        description=description,
        agent=agent,
        expected_output="Result from A2A delegation",
        input_files=input_files or {},
    )

    def task_to_kickoff_adapter(
        self: Any, task: Task, context: str | None, tools: list[Any] | None
    ) -> str:
        result = original_kickoff(messages, response_format, input_files)
        return result.raw

    result_str = _execute_task_with_a2a(
        self=agent,  # type: ignore[arg-type]
        a2a_agents=a2a_agents,
        original_fn=task_to_kickoff_adapter,
        task=fake_task,
        agent_response_model=agent_response_model,
        context=None,
        tools=None,
        extension_registry=extension_registry,
    )

    return LiteAgentOutput(
        raw=result_str,
        pydantic=None,
        agent_role=agent.role,
        usage_metrics=None,
        messages=[],
    )


class LiteAgent(FlowTrackable, BaseModel):
    """
    A lightweight agent that can process messages and use tools.

    .. deprecated::
        LiteAgent is deprecated and will be removed in a future version.
        Use ``Agent().kickoff(messages)`` instead, which provides the same
        functionality with additional features like memory and knowledge support.

    This agent is simpler than the full Agent class, focusing on direct execution
    rather than task delegation. It's designed to be used for simple interactions
    where a full crew is not needed.

    Attributes:
        role: The role of the agent.
        goal: The objective of the agent.
        backstory: The backstory of the agent.
        llm: The language model that will run the agent.
        tools: Tools at the agent's disposal.
        verbose: Whether the agent execution should be in verbose mode.
        max_iterations: Maximum number of iterations for tool usage.
        max_execution_time: Maximum execution time in seconds.
        response_format: Optional Pydantic model for structured output.
    """

    model_config = {"arbitrary_types_allowed": True}
    id: UUID4 = Field(default_factory=uuid.uuid4, frozen=True)
    role: str = Field(description="Role of the agent")
    goal: str = Field(description="Goal of the agent")
    backstory: str = Field(description="Backstory of the agent")
    llm: str | InstanceOf[BaseLLM] | Any | None = Field(
        default=None, description="Language model that will run the agent"
    )
    tools: list[BaseTool] = Field(
        default_factory=list, description="Tools at agent's disposal"
    )
    max_iterations: int = Field(
        default=15, description="Maximum number of iterations for tool usage"
    )
    max_execution_time: int | None = Field(
        default=None, description=". Maximum execution time in seconds"
    )
    respect_context_window: bool = Field(
        default=True,
```

### 0118 TOOL OUTPUT `shell_command`

```text
Exit code: 0
Wall time: 0.8 seconds
Output:
from __future__ import annotations

import json
from pathlib import Path
from time import perf_counter

from crewai import Agent
from pydantic import BaseModel, Field

from automated_research_report_generator_v0_1.crew import get_llm
from automated_research_report_generator_v0_1.tools.pdf_page_tools import (
    PdfPageIndexEntry,
    build_page_index_payload,
    default_page_index_path,
    extract_pdf_pages,
    page_index_is_current,
    reset_pdf_page_tool_runtime_state,
    save_page_index,
    set_pdf_context,
)


# =========================
# Page Index Agent Parameters
# =========================

PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_ROLE = "PDF 逐页索引专员"  # 默认角色名；可改成更贴近你内部分工的中文称呼。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_GOAL = (  # 默认目标；可改成更强调“筛页”或“目录化索引”的版本。
    "逐页读取 PDF，并为每一页生成一个简短主题标签，帮助后续 agent 快速判断哪些页与自己的分析任务相关。"
)
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_BACKSTORY = (  # 默认背景设定；可改成更偏招股书、年报或行业报告场景。
    "你专门负责按页阅读 PDF。你不会跨页总结，也不会提前做整份文档分析。"
    "你的唯一职责是只根据当前这一页的内容，输出一个非常短、便于筛页的主题标签。"
)
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TEMPERATURE = 0.1  # 默认 0.1；可改到 0 更稳，0.2-0.3 会更灵活但更易漂移。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_VERBOSE = True  # 默认 True；调试时方便看 agent 过程，可改 False 收敛日志。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_ALLOW_DELEGATION = False  # 默认 False；该 agent 只做单页索引，不需要委派。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_REASONING = False  # 默认 False；该任务短且结构化，通常不需要额外 reasoning。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_CACHE = True  # 默认 True；相同输入可复用缓存，减少重复调用。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS = 20  # 逐页短调用不应该无限等到底层默认 600 秒。
PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_MAX_RETRIES = 0  # 单页失败直接走启发式兜底，避免一次卡住后再重试。


# =========================
# Page Index Task Parameters
# =========================

PAGE_INDEX_TOPIC_MAX_CHARS = 10  # 默认主题最长 10 字；可调大到 12-15 字换取更完整标签。
PAGE_INDEX_UNKNOWN_COMPANY = "未知公司"  # 默认公司占位值；上游没识别出公司时用于 prompt。
PAGE_INDEX_EMPTY_PAGE_TOPIC = "空白页"  # 默认空白页标签；可改成“扫描页”“图片页”等更贴近团队习惯的词。
PAGE_INDEX_FORCE_REBUILD_DEFAULT = False  # 默认优先复用缓存；改成 True 会每次都强制重建索引。
PAGE_INDEX_PROMPT_RULES = (  # 默认任务规则；可逐条增删来调整主题标签风格。
    "只输出一个 `topic` 字段。",
    f"`topic` 最多 {PAGE_INDEX_TOPIC_MAX_CHARS} 个字。",
    "只关注当前这一页，不要总结整份文档。",
    "尽量使用具体的业务主题，不要使用空泛表述。",
    "如果本页主要是表格，就概括表格的主题。",
    "如果本页难以判断，就返回一个谨慎、简短的主题。",
    "不要输出解释、前后缀、Markdown 代码块或额外文本。",
)

# =========================
# Page Index Models
# =========================

class PageTopicSummary(BaseModel):
    topic: str = Field(..., description="当前页的简短主题标签")  # 单页主题字段，供后续 agent 快速筛页。


# =========================
# Page Index Helpers
# =========================

def _normalize_topic(topic: str, fallback: str) -> str:  # 清洗 LLM 或启发式产出的主题，统一成稳定短标签。
    normalized = " ".join((topic or "").split())
    normalized = normalized.replace('"', "").replace("'", "").replace("`", "").strip(" ,.;:()[]{}")
    compact = normalized.replace(" ", "").lower()
    if compact in {"json", "{", "}", "topic", "none", "null"}:
        normalized = ""
    if not normalized:
        normalized = fallback
    return normalized[:PAGE_INDEX_TOPIC_MAX_CHARS]


def _heuristic_topic(page_text: str, fallback: str) -> str:  # LLM 失败时退化为“取首个像标题的文本”。
    for line in page_text.splitlines():
        cleaned = " ".join(line.split()).strip(" ,.;:()[]{}")
        if len(cleaned) >= 2:
            return _normalize_topic(cleaned, fallback)
    return fallback


def _extract_topic_from_raw(raw: str) -> str:  # 兼容模型偶发返回 fenced JSON 或裸 JSON 的情况。
    cleaned = (raw or "").strip()
    if not cleaned:
        return ""

    if cleaned.startswith("```"):
        cleaned = cleaned.strip("`").strip()
        if cleaned.lower().startswith("json"):
            cleaned = cleaned[4:].strip()

    try:
        data = json.loads(cleaned)
    except Exception:
        return cleaned

    if isinstance(data, dict):
        return str(data.get("topic", "") or "")
    return ""


def build_page_topic_task_prompt(page_number: int, page_text: str, company_name: str = "") -> str:  # 把“单页主题摘要任务”的提示词集中到一处，便于单独调试。
    prompt_parts = [
        "你是一个投行初级分析师，负责给一页 PDF 打一个简短主题标签。",
        "",
        "规则：",
    ]
    prompt_parts.extend(f"- {rule}" for rule in PAGE_INDEX_PROMPT_RULES)
    prompt_parts.extend(
        [
            "",
            f"公司名称：{company_name or PAGE_INDEX_UNKNOWN_COMPANY}",
            f"页码：{page_number}",
            f"当前页文本：{page_text}",
        ]
    )
    return "\n".join(prompt_parts).strip()


# =========================
# Page Index Agent
# =========================

def create_page_indexer_agent() -> Agent:  # 专门负责“逐页读 PDF 并生成短主题”的独立 agent。
    return Agent(
        role=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_ROLE,  # 默认“PDF 逐页索引专员”；可改成更贴近你内部角色定义的名字。
        goal=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_GOAL,  # 默认聚焦“逐页筛页”；可改成更强调招股书目录化摘要。
        backstory=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_BACKSTORY,  # 默认强调“不跨页总结”；可按文档类型微调语境。
        llm=get_llm(
            temperature=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TEMPERATURE,
            timeout=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS,
            max_retries=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_MAX_RETRIES,
        ),  # 逐页预处理要快失败快回退，避免单页卡 10 分钟。
        verbose=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_VERBOSE,  # 默认 True；调试索引过程时保留详细日志。
        allow_delegation=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_ALLOW_DELEGATION,  # 默认 False；逐页摘要任务通常不需要委派。
        reasoning=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_REASONING,  # 默认 False；结构化短任务通常不需要 reasoning。
        cache=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_CACHE,  # 默认 True；相同 prompt 可复用缓存。
        max_retry_limit=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_MAX_RETRIES,
    )

# =========================
# Page Index Task Execution
# =========================

def summarize_page_topic(  # 对单页执行一次摘要任务，输出页码到主题的结构化映射。
    agent: Agent,
    page_number: int,
    page_text: str,
    company_name: str = "",  # 默认空字符串；上游识别出公司名时传入可提升主题稳定性。
) -> PdfPageIndexEntry:
    fallback = PAGE_INDEX_EMPTY_PAGE_TOPIC if not page_text.strip() else f"第{page_number}页"  # 默认空白页用固定标签，非空页则回退为页码标签。
    if not page_text.strip():
        return PdfPageIndexEntry(page_number=page_number, topic=fallback)

    prompt = build_page_topic_task_prompt(page_number=page_number, page_text=page_text, company_name=company_name)  # 先集中生成任务 prompt，方便调试时单独打印。
    started_at = perf_counter()

    try:
        result = agent.kickoff(prompt, response_format=PageTopicSummary)  # 优先用 CrewAI 结构化输出，避免手工猜 JSON。
        topic = ""
        if getattr(result, "pydantic", None):
            topic = str(result.pydantic.topic or "")
        if not topic:
            topic = _extract_topic_from_raw(getattr(result, "raw", "") or "")
        elapsed_seconds = perf_counter() - started_at
        print(f"[PDF Index] page {page_number} completed in {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s")
    except Exception as exc:
        elapsed_seconds = perf_counter() - started_at
        print(
            "[PDF Index] page "
            f"{page_number} failed after {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s with "
            f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}"
        )
        topic = _heuristic_topic(page_text, fallback)  # 模型失败时退回启发式标题抽取，保证索引流程不中断。

    return PdfPageIndexEntry(
        page_number=page_number,
        topic=_normalize_topic(str(topic), fallback),
    )


# =========================
# Page Index Entrypoint
# =========================

def ensure_pdf_page_index(  # 页索引总入口：优先复用最新 JSON，必要时才重建整本 PDF 的页索引。
    pdf_file_path: str,
    company_name: str = "",  # 默认空字符串；传入公司名可让逐页主题标注更贴近业务语境。
    force_rebuild: bool = PAGE_INDEX_FORCE_REBUILD_DEFAULT,  # 默认 False；改 True 时忽略缓存，强制重建整本索引。
) -> str:
    pdf_path = Path(pdf_file_path).expanduser().resolve()
    if not pdf_path.exists():
        raise FileNotFoundError(f"PDF file does not exist: {pdf_path}")

    index_path = default_page_index_path(pdf_path)  # 固定索引文件名，便于用户和 agent 稳定引用。
    if not force_rebuild and page_index_is_current(pdf_path, index_path):
        set_pdf_context(str(pdf_path), str(index_path))
        return str(index_path)

    pages = extract_pdf_pages(pdf_path)  # 先抽出每一页的纯文本，再逐页做主题标注。
    page_indexer = create_page_indexer_agent()  # 把 agent 创建放在入口里，方便后续单独替换配置。
    page_entries: list[PdfPageIndexEntry] = []

    for page_number, page_text in enumerate(pages, start=1):
        print(f"[PDF Index] summarizing page {page_number}/{len(pages)}")
        page_entries.append(
            summarize_page_topic(
                agent=page_indexer,
                page_number=page_number,
                page_text=page_text,
                company_name=company_name,
            )
        )

    payload = build_page_index_payload(pdf_path, page_entries)  # 写盘前补齐 PDF 名称、指纹和生成时间等元数据。
    saved_index_path = save_page_index(payload, index_path)  # 把最终页索引 JSON 写入 .cache。
    set_pdf_context(str(pdf_path), saved_index_path)  # 更新共享上下文，让后续工具直接复用这份索引。
    return saved_index_path


# =========================
# Shared Runtime Reset
# =========================

def reset_pdf_preprocessing_runtime_state() -> None:  # 运行前清理共享 PDF 页面工具的内存态，但保留 .cache 磁盘缓存。
    reset_pdf_page_tool_runtime_state()


def reset_pdf_indexing_runtime_state() -> None:  # 兼容旧调用名；实际清理的是预处理阶段共享的 PDF 页面缓存。
    reset_pdf_preprocessing_runtime_state()
```

# =========================
# Shared Prompt / Output Parameters
# =========================

PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_UNKNOWN_COMPANY = "鏈煡鍏徃"
PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_EMPTY_PAGE_TOPIC = "绌虹櫧椤?

    "鍙緭鍑轰竴涓?`topic` 瀛楁銆?,
    f"`topic` 鏈€澶?{PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_TOPIC_MAX_CHARS} 涓瓧銆?,

    "濡傛灉鏈〉闅句互鍒ゆ柇锛屽氨杩斿洖涓€涓皑鎱庛€佺畝鐭殑涓婚銆?,
    "涓嶈杈撳嚭瑙ｉ噴銆佸墠鍚庣紑銆丮arkdown 浠ｇ爜鍧楁垨棰濆鏂囨湰銆?,
)


class ParallelPageTopicSummary(BaseModel):
    topic: str = Field(..., description="褰撳墠椤电殑绠€鐭富棰樻爣绛?)


def _normalize_topic(topic: str, fallback: str) -> str:
    normalized = " ".join((topic or "").split())
    normalized = normalized.replace('"', "").replace("'", "").replace("`", "").strip(" ,.;:()[]{}")
    compact = normalized.replace(" ", "").lower()
    if compact in {"json", "{", "}", "topic", "none", "null"}:
        normalized = ""
    if not normalized:
        normalized = fallback
    return normalized[:PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_TOPIC_MAX_CHARS]


def _heuristic_topic(page_text: str, fallback: str) -> str:
    for line in page_text.splitlines():
        cleaned = " ".join(line.split()).strip(" ,.;:()[]{}")
        if len(cleaned) >= 2:
            return _normalize_topic(cleaned, fallback)
    return fallback


def _extract_topic_from_raw(raw: str) -> str:
    cleaned = (raw or "").strip()
    if not cleaned:
        return ""

    if cleaned.startswith("```"):
        cleaned = cleaned.strip("`").strip()
        if cleaned.lower().startswith("json"):
            cleaned = cleaned[4:].strip()

    try:
        data = json.loads(cleaned)
    except Exception:
        return cleaned

    if isinstance(data, dict):
        return str(data.get("topic", "") or "")
    return ""


def _extract_topic_from_result(result: object) -> str:
    topic = ""
    if getattr(result, "pydantic", None):
        topic = str(result.pydantic.topic or "")
    if not topic:
        topic = _extract_topic_from_raw(getattr(result, "raw", "") or "")
    return topic


def _read_int_env(name: str, default: int, minimum: int = 1) -> int:
    raw = os.getenv(name, "").strip()
    if not raw:
        return default

    try:
        return max(minimum, int(raw))
    except ValueError:
        return default


def get_parallel_page_index_max_concurrency() -> int:
    return _read_int_env(
        "PDF_INDEX_PARALLEL_MAX_CONCURRENCY",
        PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY_DEFAULT,
        minimum=1,
    )


def get_parallel_page_index_retry_limit() -> int:
    return _read_int_env(
        "PDF_INDEX_PARALLEL_RETRY_LIMIT",
        PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_LIMIT_DEFAULT,
        minimum=0,
    )


def _is_retryable_page_index_error(exc: Exception) -> bool:
    error_text = f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}".lower()
    retryable_markers = (
        "429",
        "rate limit",
        "too many requests",
        "timeout",
        "timed out",
        "connection",
        "temporarily unavailable",
        "bad gateway",
        "gateway timeout",
        "service unavailable",
        "502",
        "503",
        "504",
    )
    return any(marker in error_text for marker in retryable_markers)


def build_parallel_page_topic_task_prompt(
    page_number: int,
    page_text: str,
    company_name: str = "",
) -> str:
    prompt_parts = [
        "浣犳槸涓€涓姇琛屽垵绾у垎鏋愬笀锛岃礋璐ｇ粰涓€椤?PDF 鎵撲竴涓畝鐭富棰樻爣绛俱€?,
        "",
        "瑙勫垯锛?,
    ]
    prompt_parts.extend(f"- {rule}" for rule in PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_PROMPT_RULES)
    prompt_parts.extend(
        [
            "",
            f"鍏徃鍚嶇О锛歿company_name or PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_UNKNOWN_COMPANY}",
            f"椤电爜锛歿page_number}",
            f"褰撳墠椤垫枃鏈細{page_text}",
        ]
    )
    return "\n".join(prompt_parts).strip()


def create_parallel_page_indexer_lite_agent() -> LiteAgent:
    return LiteAgent(
        role=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_ROLE,
        goal=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_GOAL,
        backstory=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_BACKSTORY,
        llm=get_llm(
            temperature=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TEMPERATURE,
            timeout=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS,
            max_retries=0,
        ),
        verbose=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_VERBOSE,
        max_execution_time=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS,
        response_format=ParallelPageTopicSummary,
    )


async def summarize_page_topic_with_lite_agent_async(
    page_number: int,
    page_text: str,
    company_name: str,
    total_pages: int,
    semaphore: asyncio.Semaphore,
) -> PdfPageIndexEntry:
    fallback = (
        PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_EMPTY_PAGE_TOPIC
        if not page_text.strip()
        else f"绗瑊page_number}椤?
    )
    if not page_text.strip():
        return PdfPageIndexEntry(page_number=page_number, topic=fallback)

    prompt = build_parallel_page_topic_task_prompt(
        page_number=page_number,
        page_text=page_text,
        company_name=company_name,
    )
    retry_limit = get_parallel_page_index_retry_limit()

    async with semaphore:
        for attempt in range(retry_limit + 1):
            started_at = perf_counter()
            try:
                result = await create_parallel_page_indexer_lite_agent().kickoff_async(
                    prompt,
                    response_format=ParallelPageTopicSummary,
                )
                topic = _extract_topic_from_result(result)
                elapsed_seconds = perf_counter() - started_at
                print(
                    f"[PDF Index Parallel] page {page_number}/{total_pages} "
                    f"completed in {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s"
                )
                return PdfPageIndexEntry(
                    page_number=page_number,
                    topic=_normalize_topic(str(topic), fallback),
                )
            except Exception as exc:
                elapsed_seconds = perf_counter() - started_at
                should_retry = attempt < retry_limit and _is_retryable_page_index_error(exc)
                if should_retry:
                    delay_seconds = PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_BASE_DELAY_SECONDS * (2 ** attempt)
                    print(
                        "[PDF Index Parallel] page "
                        f"{page_number}/{total_pages} failed after {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s with "
                        f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}. "
                        f"Retrying in {delay_seconds:.1f}s "
                        f"({attempt + 1}/{retry_limit})"
                    )
                    await asyncio.sleep(delay_seconds)
                    continue

                print(
                    "[PDF Index Parallel] page "
                    f"{page_number}/{total_pages} failed after {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s with "
                    f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}"
                )
                return PdfPageIndexEntry(
                    page_number=page_number,
                    topic=_heuristic_topic(page_text, fallback),
                )

    return PdfPageIndexEntry(page_number=page_number, topic=fallback)


async def summarize_pages_with_parallel_lite_agent(
    pages: list[str],
    company_name: str = "",
    max_concurrency: int = PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY_DEFAULT,
) -> list[PdfPageIndexEntry]:
    semaphore = asyncio.Semaphore(max_concurrency)
    total_pages = len(pages)
    tasks = [
        summarize_page_topic_with_lite_agent_async(
            page_number=page_number,
            page_text=page_text,
            company_name=company_name,
            total_pages=total_pages,
            semaphore=semaphore,
        )
        for page_number, page_text in enumerate(pages, start=1)
    ]
    return await asyncio.gather(*tasks)


def ensure_pdf_page_index_parallel(
    pdf_file_path: str,
    company_name: str = "",
    force_rebuild: bool = PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_FORCE_REBUILD_DEFAULT,
) -> str:
    pdf_path = Path(pdf_file_path).expanduser().resolve()
    if not pdf_path.exists():
        raise FileNotFoundError(f"PDF file does not exist: {pdf_path}")

    index_path = default_page_index_path(pdf_path)
    if not force_rebuild and page_index_is_current(pdf_path, index_path):
        set_pdf_context(str(pdf_path), str(index_path))
        return str(index_path)

    pages = extract_pdf_pages(pdf_path)
    max_concurrency = get_parallel_page_index_max_concurrency()
    print(
        "[PDF Index Parallel] using bounded concurrency "
        f"(max_concurrency={max_concurrency}, pages={len(pages)})"
    )
    page_entries = asyncio.run(
        summarize_pages_with_parallel_lite_agent(
            pages=pages,
            company_name=company_name,
            max_concurrency=max_concurrency,
        )
    )

    payload = build_page_index_payload(pdf_path, page_entries)
    saved_index_path = save_page_index(payload, index_path)
    set_pdf_context(str(pdf_path), saved_index_path)
    return saved_index_path
```

63	class ParallelPageTopicSummary(BaseModel):
64	    topic: str = Field(..., description="褰撳墠椤电殑绠€鐭富棰樻爣绛?)
65	
66	
67	def _normalize_topic(topic: str, fallback: str) -> str:
68	    normalized = " ".join((topic or "").split())
69	    normalized = normalized.replace('"', "").replace("'", "").replace("`", "").strip(" ,.;:()[]{}")
70	    compact = normalized.replace(" ", "").lower()
71	    if compact in {"json", "{", "}", "topic", "none", "null"}:
72	        normalized = ""
73	    if not normalized:
74	        normalized = fallback
75	    return normalized[:PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_TOPIC_MAX_CHARS]
76	
77	
78	def _heuristic_topic(page_text: str, fallback: str) -> str:
79	    for line in page_text.splitlines():
80	        cleaned = " ".join(line.split()).strip(" ,.;:()[]{}")
81	        if len(cleaned) >= 2:
82	            return _normalize_topic(cleaned, fallback)
83	    return fallback
84	
85	
86	def _extract_topic_from_raw(raw: str) -> str:
87	    cleaned = (raw or "").strip()
88	    if not cleaned:
89	        return ""
90	
91	    if cleaned.startswith("```"):
92	        cleaned = cleaned.strip("`").strip()
93	        if cleaned.lower().startswith("json"):
94	            cleaned = cleaned[4:].strip()
95	
96	    try:
97	        data = json.loads(cleaned)
98	    except Exception:
99	        return cleaned
100	
101	    if isinstance(data, dict):
102	        return str(data.get("topic", "") or "")
103	    return ""
104	
105	
106	def _extract_topic_from_result(result: object) -> str:
107	    topic = ""
108	    if getattr(result, "pydantic", None):
109	        topic = str(result.pydantic.topic or "")
110	    if not topic:
111	        topic = _extract_topic_from_raw(getattr(result, "raw", "") or "")
112	    return topic
113	
114	
115	def _read_int_env(name: str, default: int, minimum: int = 1) -> int:
116	    raw = os.getenv(name, "").strip()
117	    if not raw:
118	        return default
119	
120	    try:
121	        return max(minimum, int(raw))
122	    except ValueError:
123	        return default
124	
125	
126	def get_parallel_page_index_max_concurrency() -> int:
127	    return _read_int_env(
128	        "PDF_INDEX_PARALLEL_MAX_CONCURRENCY",
129	        PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY_DEFAULT,
130	        minimum=1,
131	    )
132	
133	
134	def get_parallel_page_index_retry_limit() -> int:
135	    return _read_int_env(
136	        "PDF_INDEX_PARALLEL_RETRY_LIMIT",
137	        PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_LIMIT_DEFAULT,
138	        minimum=0,
139	    )
140	
141	
142	def _is_retryable_page_index_error(exc: Exception) -> bool:
143	    error_text = f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}".lower()
144	    retryable_markers = (
145	        "429",
146	        "rate limit",
147	        "too many requests",
148	        "timeout",
149	        "timed out",
150	        "connection",
151	        "temporarily unavailable",
152	        "bad gateway",
153	        "gateway timeout",
154	        "service unavailable",
155	        "502",
156	        "503",
157	        "504",
158	    )
159	    return any(marker in error_text for marker in retryable_markers)
160

162	def build_parallel_page_topic_task_prompt(
163	    page_number: int,
164	    page_text: str,
165	    company_name: str = "",
166	) -> str:
167	    prompt_parts = [
168	        "浣犳槸涓€涓姇琛屽垵绾у垎鏋愬笀锛岃礋璐ｇ粰涓€椤?PDF 鎵撲竴涓畝鐭富棰樻爣绛俱€?,
169	        "",
170	        "瑙勫垯锛?,
171	    ]
172	    prompt_parts.extend(f"- {rule}" for rule in PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_PROMPT_RULES)
173	    prompt_parts.extend(
174	        [
175	            "",

178	            f"褰撳墠椤垫枃鏈細{page_text}",
179	        ]
180	    )
181	    return "\n".join(prompt_parts).strip()

192	            max_retries=0,
193	        ),
194	        verbose=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_VERBOSE,
195	        max_execution_time=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS,
196	        response_format=ParallelPageTopicSummary,
197	    )

200	async def summarize_page_topic_with_lite_agent_async(
201	    page_number: int,
202	    page_text: str,
203	    company_name: str,
204	    total_pages: int,
205	    semaphore: asyncio.Semaphore,

207	    fallback = (

235	                )
236	                return PdfPageIndexEntry(
237	                    page_number=page_number,
238	                    topic=_normalize_topic(str(topic), fallback),
239	                )
240	            except Exception as exc:
241	                elapsed_seconds = perf_counter() - started_at
242	                should_retry = attempt < retry_limit and _is_retryable_page_index_error(exc)
243	                if should_retry:
244	                    delay_seconds = PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_BASE_DELAY_SECONDS * (2 ** attempt)
245	                    print(
246	                        "[PDF Index Parallel] page "
247	                        f"{page_number}/{total_pages} failed after {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s with "
248	                        f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}. "

251	                    )
252	                    await asyncio.sleep(delay_seconds)
253	                    continue
254	
255	                print(
256	                    "[PDF Index Parallel] page "
257	                    f"{page_number}/{total_pages} failed after {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s with "
258	                    f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}"
259	                )
260	                return PdfPageIndexEntry(
261	                    page_number=page_number,
262	                    topic=_heuristic_topic(page_text, fallback),
263	                )
264	
265	    return PdfPageIndexEntry(page_number=page_number, topic=fallback)
266	
267	
268	async def summarize_pages_with_parallel_lite_agent(
269	    pages: list[str],
270	    company_name: str = "",
271	    max_concurrency: int = PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY_DEFAULT,

282	        )
283	        for page_number, page_text in enumerate(pages, start=1)
284	    ]
285	    return await asyncio.gather(*tasks)
